## Rollback Instructions
To rollback to a specific checkpoint:
```bash
# List all checkpoints
git tag -l checkpoint-* | sort -r

# List GitHub releases
gh release list

# Rollback to a checkpoint
git checkout checkpoint-YYYYMMDD-HHMMSS
```
